	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　そして何より。あの事件への関心が再び呼び起こされ、…風化されないことを何より強く願う。",
		   NULL, "And more importantly: that nothing like this ever happens again.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();


//　最後のあとがきにはこう記した￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　最後のあとがきにはこう記した。",
		   NULL, "I wrote this in the afterword:", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();


//　この惨劇が、どうして起こされたのか＠
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 13, "ps3/s05/13/101300788", 128, TRUE);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(5, 11, "ps3/s05/11/100700877", 128, TRUE);
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_Continue); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　この惨劇が、どうして起こされたのか。",
		   NULL, "Why did this tragedy happen?", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　私たちだけでは真相に至ることがかないません＠
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 13, "ps3/s05/13/101300789", 128, TRUE);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(5, 11, "ps3/s05/11/100700878", 128, TRUE);
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_Continue); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　私たちだけでは真相に至ることがかないません。",
		   NULL, "We can't reach the truth by ourselves.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　どうかこれを読んだあなた＠
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 13, "ps3/s05/13/101300790", 128, TRUE);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(5, 11, "ps3/s05/11/100700879", 128, TRUE);
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_Continue); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　どうかこれを読んだあなた。",
		   NULL, "If you're reading this.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　真相を解き明かしてください＠
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 13, "ps3/s05/13/101300791", 128, TRUE);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(5, 11, "ps3/s05/11/100700880", 128, TRUE);
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_Continue); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　真相を解き明かしてください。",
		   NULL, "Please discover the truth.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　それだけが私たちの願いです＠
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 13, "ps3/s05/13/101300792", 128, TRUE);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(5, 11, "ps3/s05/11/100700881", 128, TRUE);
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_Continue); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　それだけが私たちの願いです。",
		   NULL, "That is our only wish.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//!s0　　　　　　　　　　　　　大石蔵人・赤坂衛!sd

	SetSpeedOfMessage( TRUE, 128, );


	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　　　　　　　　　　　　　大石蔵人・赤坂衛",
		   NULL, "Kuraudo Ooishi, Mamoru Akasaka.", Line_Normal);

	ClearMessage();
	SetSpeedOfMessage( FALSE, 0, );


	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 2000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

//locate 0,7

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode) == 0) { SetDrawingPointOfMessage( 0, 7 ); }

//雛見沢地区の封鎖は、今年もまだ解けていない￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "雛見沢地区の封鎖は、今年もまだ解けていない。",
		   NULL, "This year, the quarantine on Hinamizawa still hasn't been lifted.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();


//※ど～～～ん！　で、『ひぐらしのなく頃に』
//＝ｗ＝）＜おつかれさま～～～☆

	FadeOutBGM( 1, 1000, FALSE );
	FadeOutBGM( 2, 1000, TRUE );
	DisableWindow();
	DrawScene("white", 50 );
	PlaySE( 3, "wa_036", 128, 64 );

//lsph 21,":c;bmp\Efe\End_2.bmp",0,0
//vsp 21,1


	DrawScene("end_1", 1500 );
	DrawScene("end_2", 1500 );
//	DrawScene( "end_3", 1500 );

//setwindow 8,16,23,16,26,26,0,2,20,1,1,#ffffff,0,0,639,479
//print 10,4000

	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	DrawBustshot(5, "black", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 4000, TRUE );

//csp -1
	DisableWindow();
	DrawScene("black", 400 );

//mov %Omake,1
//mov %Himatubusi_END,1
//mov %NEW_bg,4

	DrawSceneWithMask("s_jump_back", "4", 0, 0, 1500 );
	PlaySE( 3, "wa_041", 128, 64 );
	DrawSceneWithMask("ex_otsu_hima", "5", 0, 0, 1500 );
	Wait( 10000 );


	DrawScene("black", 1000 );
